>> New-ItemProperty -Path HKLM:\SYSTEM\CurrentControlSet\Control\FileSystem `
>>   -Name LongPathsEnabled -Value 1 -PropertyType DWord -Force
>>
>> # 1) Allow long paths in Git (admin shell):
>> git config --system core.longpaths true
>>
>> # 2) Ensure credentials are clean and in-console:
>> git config --global --unset credential.helper
>> git config --global credential.helper manager
>> git config --global credential.guiPrompt false
>> git config --global core.pager cat
>>
>> # 3) Commit/push again from CoCache:
>> cd "$env:USERPROFILE\Documents\GitHub\CoCache"
>> git add -A
>> git commit -m "Resume ingest after long-path fix"
>> git push
>>
